<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развивать.html>развива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развиваться.html>развива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развиться.html>разви́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to develop <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to progress</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развиваться.html>развива́ются</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́я</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Déti <b>razvivájutsja</b> igrája.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Children develop while playing</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to untwist; to come unwound; to come uncurled, to lose its curl <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of hair</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развивать.html>развива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развить.html>разви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развиться.html>разви́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развиваться.html>развива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to develop <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to progress</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развиваться.html>развива́ются</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́я</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Déti <b>razvivájutsja</b> igrája.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Children develop while playing</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to untwist; to come unwound; to come uncurled, to lose its curl <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of hair</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развить.html>разви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вле<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тель<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развод.html>разво́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развод.html>разво́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развод.html>разво́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развод.html>разво́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>divorce</li>
<li>opening, raising, swinging open
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:развод.html>разво́д</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мост.html>мосто́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvód</b> mostóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>raising</b> the bridges</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> relief, mounting, posting</li>
<li>breeding</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> free designs, broad pattern</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stains</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> scam, cheating
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развод.html>разво́да</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сайт.html>са́йтах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знакомство.html>знако́мств</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:общение.html>обще́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посетитель.html>посети́телем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:робот.html>ро́ботов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нанятый.html>на́нятых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>люде́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мени</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:реальный.html>реа́льных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:желающий.html>жела́ющих</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:познакомиться.html>познако́миться</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Variánt <b>razvóda</b> na sájtax znakómstv — obščénije s posetítelem róbotov íli nánjatyx ljudéj ot ímeni reálʹnyx želájuščix poznakómitʹsja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">One kind of dating site <b>scam</b> is the use of bots or hired personnel to talk to a user while pretending to be real people interested in dating.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

***разводить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разводить.html>разводи́ть</a> (4855)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разводить.html>разводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развести.html>развести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take along, to bring; to conduct</li>
<li>to part, to move apart, to pull apart, to separate</li>
<li>to dilute, to mix</li>
<li>to dissolve</li>
<li>to start</li>
<li>to divorce</li>
<li>to mount, to relieve, to post (sentinels)</li>
<li>to rear, to breed (animals)</li>
<li>to plant, to cultivate, to grow (plants)</li>
<li>to make, to plant, to lay out (a park, garden, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cheat, to swindle</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развод.html>разво́д</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvód</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разво́дка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvódka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разводиться.html>разводи́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvodítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть</b>

</p>
<ol><li>to be divorced, to divorce, to obtain a divorce <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<li>to grow in number, to breed</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разводить.html>разводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства_2"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:развестись.html>развести́сь</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>раз-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-вод-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развозить.html>развози́ть</a> (17675)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развозить.html>развози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развезти.html>развезти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deliver, to transport (multiple people or things to their respective destinations)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make impassable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развозить.html>разво́зит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dorógu <b>razvózit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the road is becoming impassable</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***разворачивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивать</a> (9920)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разворотить.html>развороти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvoráčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разворотить.html>развороти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to unroll, to unwind, to unfold, to unwrap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ковер.html>ковёр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvoráčivatʹ</b> kovjór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unroll a carpet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:газета.html>газе́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvoráčivatʹ</b> gazétu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unfold the paper</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пакет.html>паке́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvoráčivatʹ</b> pakét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unwrap a parcel</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знамя.html>знамёна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvoráčivatʹ</b> znamjóna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spread out the banners</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to show, to display
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvoráčivatʹ</b> svoí síly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show/display/reveal one's strength</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvoráčivatʹ</b> svoj talánt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show/display one's talent</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to start <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvoráčivatʹ</b> svojó délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to start up a business of one's own</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put on a wide scale, to widen, to broaden, to expand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:торговля.html>торго́влю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvoráčivatʹ</b> torgóvlju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to expand trade</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deploy, to extend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to expand <i>(into)</i></li>
<li>to turn, to swing about, to swing around, to slew <i>(about)</i>, to make a U-turn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́ну</a> <b><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивает</a></strong></b> поперёк <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mašínu <b>razvoráčivajet</b> poperjók dorógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the car is <b>veering</b> across the road</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to play havoc <i>(among, with)</i>, to turn upside down
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разворотить.html>развороти́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачиваться.html>развора́чиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvoráčivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуться.html>разверну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn around, to swing about / around; to make a U-turn (vehicle); to slew (about)</li>
<li>to be deployed (of troops) = <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развертываться.html>развёртываться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvjórtyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li>to come unrolled / unfolded / unwrapped = <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развертываться.html>развёртываться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvjórtyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li>to spread, to expand</li>
<li>to display oneself</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvoráčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ра́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:развернуться.html>разверну́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>раз-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-ворач-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ива</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачиваться.html>развора́чивающийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvoráčivajuščijsja</span>)
